My first visit to this breathtaking venue was last week 20 May 2021 for a truly beautiful wedding. The happy couple chose this place wisely. The views were lovely. The on-site staff were super friendly and helpful and attentive. Only complaint: the waitstaff could use a lot of training about clearing tables.
The ceremony was outside with a view of the neighbouring vineyard as was the cocktail area.
The dining room was a great size and opened up into a couple of courtyards. There were picturesque spots and staged seating areas with chandeliers all over the grounds. It was so well thought out.
We eat and danced and laughed and celebrated with adorable bride and groom until the evening.   It couldn‚Äôt have been a better day if we tried! Well done, Villa de Amore!</review>

< Text>
We are so happy to have chosen Villa De Amore as our venue to celebrate our wedding and reception.  Elegant, beautiful, and joy-filled is how I'd explain and alway remember our experience. From the moment we arrived to the sweet finish of the grand exit, we were catered to and cared for.

The property is beautiful, and despite being early season for a wedding, the grounds and surrounding vineyards presented themselves majestically. The rolling hills and blue skies painted the perfect backdrop for our nuptials, followed by a glorious sunset into night for cake cutting and dancing. The vendors Villa De Amore works with are also fantastic! 5 stars is not enough. Exceptional.< /Text>

Absolutely beautiful wedding venue!!! My fiance and I are so excited to get married here next year. < Review>
Future brides and grooms, RUN and DO NOT look back!! I like to echo all the couples who had a horrible experience with Villa De Amore during this time. My husband and I were supposed to get married in late June and of course, that did not happen because of the pandemic. Your wedding is supposed to be the happiest and joyful event in your life, however, dealing with Eileen and David during this pandemic was nothing, but STRESS and HEADACHES. They claim to be a family owned business, but unfortunately, all they care about is money!

We reached out to Villa De Amore in March of 2020, three months before our wedding, expressing our concerns about if our wedding was going to happen in June. If it was not going to happen as it states in our contract, we were looking for a refund and not a postponement.
David stated that he did not know if they could have our wedding, but told us to wait until 30 days prior to our wedding date for his decision. We had also asked if they would honor their force majeure in their contact, and at the time, David said their insurance would review our claim. This gave us hope that would honor this clause in our contract.  As the days and months went by, cases of Covid continued to rise and it didn‚Äôt look like we would be able to hold our wedding. In May, a few days before we hit the 30-day mark, I called Riverside County and they confirmed with me that NO businesses were allowed to conduct weddings at that time. I also called a few wineries in Temecula, and ALL of them said they have already postponed or refunded all their couples. Once again, I reached out to David and Eileen about what Riverside County and other wineries had said and done, but again, they said they do not know whether they could hold our wedding and also added, that they WILL NOT refund our money and that our only option is to choose an undesirable date for the future (in my opinion). Our wedding is a destination wedding for us and the majority of our guests, so we were not going to risk their safety in having our wedding there. What was even worse, was that two weeks prior to our wedding, Eileen had the nerve to email us and said that they got the okay to hold our wedding and send them our final count. As we all know now and back then, we were clearly still in the middle of the pandemic, and weddings were still not allowed at that time! At this point, we knew we could not trust them. During this time, they did nothing, but misled us with false information and acted as if they were above the law as they decided not to listen to the state and county orders. We clearly DID NOT continue our business with them and hired a lawyer. In July, we were notified that Villa De Amore had a Temporary Restraining Order from Riverside County stating that they were to stop holding, offering, and hosting wedding receptions. Also that the court finds that Villa De Amore was an immediate threat to the public‚Äôs health.

Take your hard-earned money elsewhere, because they sure do not care about you, your family, and your friend‚Äôs safety! If I could go back in time, I WOULD NEVER have trusted Villa De Amore to have my once and lifetime wedding. You deserve better!!<//Review>

<Rating>5</Rating><text>When I see 5 star reviews, my expectations already start high, so I was expecting 5 star service, but what this place delivered was beyond that. You‚Äôd think if a business did the same thing over and over again, they may get complacent or ‚Äúgo through the motions‚Äù which is the vibe I got from some other venues I‚Äôve seen, but from this place‚Ä¶never‚Ä¶not ONCE.
The moment I stepped foot on the beautiful grounds, I was in love. Even on a rainy day, the villa was breathtaking.  The owner, Elaine was super sweet, and excited to be taking me on this tour. When she was talking about her family run business (daughter and son in law in charge of catering and son is the manager) she was just bursting with enthusiasm. She was excited when she was talking about the endless inventory she acquires almost weekly to help decorate the grounds for your wedding day‚Ä¶ then, we even shared a teary moment together when I talked about my day. This. Was. It.
Then the cost‚Ä¶ all inclusive!! Photography, cake, flowers, decorations, decor, day of coordinator (who is absolutely the best by the way), wedding design, catering, bar tenders, servers, officiant, DJ, linens, all covered!!! You will not be disappointed in their amazing choice in vendors.
The Food.. AMAZING? We expected the food to be great but we were BLOWN away with how yummy it all was. We settled on Steak and Swordfish for our entrees and Shrimp Sliders, crab deviled eggs and a cheese display for appetizers. All my guests are still telling me how much they loved those Shrimp sliders. When they placed my husband's steak in front of him and my swordfish it was HUGE. That rarely happens to get amazing food and huge portions. I made SURE I ate it. Laura, the wedding day of coordinator (did I mention she‚Äôs the absolute best) was clear to make sure we knew we had 10 minutes to eat before the next thing.. so I definitely ate mine and some of my husband‚Äôs. She made sure we always had something to drink and was catering to our every need without us even having to ask her to, she literally just knew.
I don't have enough room to mention each vendor individually even though I want to, so I'll just say the florist, photographer, the DJ, the cake baker, were all on point and amazing. I did separate reviews on their websites if you want to check it out!
Bar- You can bring your own drinks! They serve them, but you bring them saving you money. I absolutely loved the way the showed off my signature drinks. The bartender stopped what he was doing when the bride needed a drink! He also ran, yes ran, when he didn‚Äôt have any apple cider at the bar and I wanted a pre-toast with my Jr. Bridesmaids.
Bury the Bourbon-We had a tradition we wanted to do where we bury the bourbon on the property one month before the wedding and to prevent it from raining on your wedding day. Our wedding was in February, it was very possible. Most venues said it wasn‚Äôt allowed. Villa‚Äôs reaction? They loved the idea. They were excited to participate in something new. My fianc√© and I paid in full to be married at Villa de Amore on April 5th, 2020- which obviously could not legally happen due to the global pandemic we are currently still enduring. The managers of this venue, Eileen Rivard and David Musser would not allow us to postpone or even reduce our guest count (which was 204 people) until Riverside county legally prohibited gatherings of more than 10 people to take place. This was only a few short weeks before our wedding. We pleaded with the owners to compromise; a staggering number of our guests were sending us regretful messages that they could not risk their lives by attending our wedding during this terrifying pandemic on a daily basis. They had no concern or sympathy for our loved ones safety- ‚Äúit‚Äôs business as usual‚Äù they said.

When they were forced by law to cancel our special day, they proceeded to offer a limited amount of undesirable dates, most of which would still be plagued with our current situation and some of which were so far out we could not wait. My fianc√©‚Äôs father was suffering from terminal illness, we needed to book a date that was far enough out for him and our other guests to be safe, but not too far as we feared his illness would take him from us before he was able to attend our wedding.

We hesitantly considered a date in august, and in response they immediately pressured us to sign new contracts. I made sure to review them to ensure the ‚Äúforce majeure‚Äù clause was present, as I was under the impression it was the only part of the original contract that protected us if this were to happen again. While going back and fourth with Eileen, I was confused about one of the first lines in the contract that addressed our refund if the anticipated amount of guests could not attend. She quickly responded that she would re-word that line to make it more clear, and a few minutes later she sent a new contract. I later found that she removed the force majeure clause, surely hoping we would have good faith that she only changed the part she claimed she would change and sign the contract without noticing.

At this point we felt massively violated. I felt these people could not be trusted. We needed to re plan our wedding quickly to ensure our beloved father could attend. We asked for the refund that their contract clearly stated we deserved, and that‚Äôs when they stopped responding all together. We emailed them constantly, and finally had no choice but to hire a lawyer. To our shock they also failed to respond to multiple correspondence from our attorney. They were well aware what we had to lose, and they were taking full advantage of it. When their lawyer responded to our attorney, the letter set forth, in my opinion, arguments that insinuated we could have foreseen COVID19 coming when we booked our wedding in May of 2019.  To me, the letter was almost as disgraceful as the venue.

We are now in the unfortunate position of having to file a lawsuit against Villa de Amore to get our money back. They claimed they were unable to refund because they needed our money to pay their staff and utilities while they have been closed and not hosting weddings. I‚Äôm curious how they planned to host our wedding on the new date they tried to have us change into if they already spent all of our money.

Our father passed away approximately two weeks ago. We are devastated that he wasn‚Äôt able to witness our wedding that we are sure he extended his life well past his prognosis for. It‚Äôs all he could talk about and he declined very quickly after it was cancelled. In my opinion, Villa de Amore made it difficult for us to plan a new wedding elsewhere in time for him to be there, and there are no words to describe our devastation over this situation.

It‚Äôs painful to re-live this experience that continues to cause us hurt and sleepless nights. I would never wish what we have been through on anyone.< /review>

<rate>5</rate>< Text>
Dave, Aimee, Eileen, Lauren, etc. with Villa de Amore were FANTASTIC, AMAZING, FLEXIBLE, HELPFUL, AFFORDABLE, etc. I really truly cannot say enough about our experience with those folks.

Venue - located in Temecula, California, about 45 min from San Diego. Needless to say, the venue is stunningly beautiful. Imagine a breathtakingly beautiful mansion on a hill with vineyards, a customized altar, a huge patio, personal dance floor, etc. - that's what you get with the villa.

Convenient - During our engagement, my husband was in Washington DC, I was in Canada, and the wedding was in California. As such, you can imagine how difficult wedding planning could be... However, it could not have been much easier, to be honest. When you meet with the villa, they give you the caterer, a choice of florists, photographers, ministers, DJ, etc etc etc. Literally all you need to do as the bride is worry about the guest list and your dress. All the vendors they allow you to choose from are professional, talented and "go out of our way" helpful.

Affordable - The fee is per guest - no hidden costs. When we did the math, they were even more affordable than other venues that you have to do piece by piece. Not only do you already have a group of vendors (cater, photo, DJ, minister, etc), but the pricing is even more affordable!

Soiree Florists - Sheila and her team over there are phenomenal. I honestly could not have made the flowers and decorations more beautiful if I tried. I told Sheila I knew nothing about flowers and just told her a group of colors. She got creative with it and on the day of the wedding, I was just blown away with the color, the styling, the artful taste - it was all amazing.

Ken Pollard - Minister - I can not say enough nice things about Ken. The man probably marries 2 couples a week - however, he still managed to make our ceremony so touching and customized to Luke and I. I don't doubt that he will be a part of our lives forever.

Overall, A++!< /Text>

<gmapID>0x80db79301a119111:0xfcc118c0736d662</gmapID><Text>Love love loved Villa de Amore.  First off, it's a family business and they really treat you like you're part of their family.  Leading up to my big day, I've called, emailed, and even showed up in person with questions/concerns and each time they were very responsive and provided me great customer service.

The venue itself is just spectacular with amazing views of grapevines surrounding the entire property.  All the detail, from the barrel wall to the newly renovated cocktail hour area with amazing chandeliers, really give it the first class quality that I loved.  And my favorite part about Villa de Amore is that you get the entire property to yourself!  There is no strangers crashing your wedding, or your guests wandering into other people's events. Everyone there is either a guest of yours or working your event.

As I mentioned before, their customer service is great.  I envisioned having an ice cream bar.  They said they have never done that before and they usually do candy bars.  But instead of telling me that an ice cream bar wasn't an option, they worked things out and made it happen!  This is just one of many requests that they fulfilled.  They truly go out of their way to accommodate your requests.  The only thing I wasn't able to do that I really wanted was a sparkler send off.  But that was due to county laws - so ladies, sorry but that's a no-go.

Another great thing about Villa de Amore is that it's sort of a one-stop-shop.  They provide all inclusive packages that includes: catering, DJ, flowers, photography, cake, minister, day-of coordinator, bartenders, personal website, props (that you can use for decor as well as for your photography sessions), and customized lighting.  I chose to use my own photographer and wanted a videographer as well as a photo booth, so I had to coordinate those myself.  But all others were minimal coordination on my part (you do have to meet with those vendors to tell them what you want but you don't have to worry about paying them separately). The unique thing about this venue is that you have to purchase your own booze (they provide the bartenders but you have to stock their bar), but the little bit of hassle that it adds to your pre-wedding-to-do-list was outweighed by the huge cost savings.  I just went to Costco and purchased a little over $1,000 worth of booze and that was way more than enough for 100 guests ($400 was suggested but we wanted top-shelf and we kind of got crazy with wanting to provide a wide selection).  Had Villa de Amore required us to purchase the booze through them (like most other venues), our bill would have easily been $4,000 and up (based on the top-shelf open bar that we did).

The cost is a bit pricey but the level of service and quality that you receive for it is worth every penny.< /Text><pics>None<//pics><username>Jill Hiraizumi< /username>< user_id>

<Review>Villa de Amore was outstanding! The venue itself is absolutely stunning. Between the landscaping, decorating, and views of the surrounding vineyards, it made for a perfect setting. In fact, because the venue had so much natural beauty to begin with, we didn't need to add many decorations!

And now for the staff- our coordinator David was great. Leading up to the wedding, he was always organized, professional, informative, quick to answer our questions via email, and flexible to meet our needs. On the wedding day, he and everyone else there were great. They were helpful and checked on us frequently without being intrusive, and they were always very friendly and patient, even if our guests were a pain at times!

Another HUGE plus was the vendors VDA uses: Leah Marie photography, Bitoni catering, Elegance on Display (baker), and Soiree (florist) were all great. The photographers were particularly awesome- Marcella and Diana were friendly, efficient, and made sure that they captured all the guest combination photos that we requested. VDA also made it easy to add our own vendors. We were especially impressed with how seamlessly VDA's DJ worked with our live band.

Now, for a couple minor negatives (it was hard to think of any!!!): it would have been nice if we or our guests could have brought home some leftovers from the caterer. The food was so good but the two of us never really got the chance to sit down and enjoy it! The only other negative is that VDA's receptions have to end at 10 pm due to local noise ordinances. This is obviously out of their control, but it is something to consider when choosing a venue.

Overall, an outstanding venue from top to bottom! We really liked the combination of the simplicity of an all-inclusive wedding along with the ability to customize things to our liking. You really can't beat this place. Thank you David, Eileen, and everyone else for the best day of our lives!< /Review><gmap_id>0x80db79301a119111:0xfcc118c0736d662< /gmap_id>< pictures>
